🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/check_editorconfig.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Script to check EditorConfig compliance for the three problematic files."""

import sys
import os

def check_file_indentation(filepath, expected_indent_style, expected_indent_size=None):
    """Check if a file uses the correct indentation style."""
    errors = []
    
    with open(filepath, '"'"'rb'"'"') as f:
        lines = f.readlines()
    
    for i, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
        # Skip empty lines
        if not line.strip():
            continue
        
        # Check for tabs vs spaces at the start of the line
        if line.startswith(b'"'"'\t'"'"'):
            if expected_indent_style == '"'"'space'"'"':
                errors.append(f"Line {i}: Found tab, expected {expected_indent_size} spaces")
        elif line.startswith(b'"'"' '"'"'):
            if expected_indent_style == '"'"'tab'"'"':
                errors.append(f"Line {i}: Found space(s), expected tab")
    
    return errors

def check_file_newline(filepath):
    """Check if a file ends with a newline."""
    with open(filepath, '"'"'rb'"'"') as f:
        f.seek(0, 2)  # Go to end
        if f.tell() > 0:
            f.seek(-1, 2)  # Go to last byte
            last_char = f.read(1)
            return last_char == b'"'"'\n'"'"'
    return True

def main():
    files_to_check = [
        {
            '"'"'path'"'"': '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"',
            '"'"'indent_style'"'"': '"'"'space'"'"',
            '"'"'indent_size'"'"': 2
        },
        {
            '"'"'path'"'"': '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"',
            '"'"'indent_style'"'"': '"'"'space'"'"',
            '"'"'indent_size'"'"': 2
        },
        {
            '"'"'path'"'"': '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'"'"',
            '"'"'indent_style'"'"': '"'"'space'"'"',  # JSON files should use spaces
            '"'"'indent_size'"'"': 2,
            '"'"'check_newline'"'"': True
        }
    ]
    
    all_errors = []
    
    for file_info in files_to_check:
        filepath = file_info['"'"'path'"'"']
        
        if not os.path.exists(filepath):
            print(f"Warning: File not found: {filepath}")
            continue
        
        print(f"\nChecking: {filepath}")
        
        # Check indentation
        errors = check_file_indentation(
            filepath,
            file_info['"'"'indent_style'"'"'],
            file_info.get('"'"'indent_size'"'"')
        )
        
        if errors:
            print(f"  Indentation errors: {len(errors)}")
            for error in errors[:5]:  # Show first 5 errors
                print(f"    - {error}")
            if len(errors) > 5:
                print(f"    ... and {len(errors) - 5} more")
            all_errors.extend(errors)
        else:
            print("  ✓ Indentation OK")
        
        # Check newline
        if file_info.get('"'"'check_newline'"'"'):
            has_newline = check_file_newline(filepath)
            if not has_newline:
                print("  ✗ Missing final newline")
                all_errors.append(f"{filepath}: Missing final newline")
            else:
                print("  ✓ Final newline OK")
    
    print(f"\n{'"'"'='"'"'*60}")
    if all_errors:
        print(f"Total errors found: {len(all_errors)}")
        return 1
    else:
        print("All files pass EditorConfig checks!")
        return 0

if __name__ == '"'"'__main__'"'"':
    sys.exit(main())

"""Script to fix EditorConfig issues in the three problematic files."""

import sys
import os

def fix_json_indentation(filepath):
    """Fix indentation in a JSON file to use 2 spaces instead of tabs."""
    with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Replace tabs with 2 spaces
    fixed_content = content.replace('"'"'\t'"'"', '"'"'  '"'"')
    
    with open(filepath, '"'"'w'"'"') as f:
        f.write(fixed_content)
    
    print(f"Fixed indentation in: {filepath}")

def add_final_newline(filepath):
    """Ensure file ends with a newline."""
    with open(filepath, '"'"'rb'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    if content and not content.endswith(b'"'"'\n'"'"'):
        with open(filepath, '"'"'ab'"'"') as f:
            f.write(b'"'"'\n'"'"')
        print(f"Added final newline to: {filepath}")
    else:
        print(f"Already has final newline: {filepath}")

def main():
    # Fix indentation in the two JSON files
    files_to_fix_indent = [
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"',
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"'
    ]
    
    for filepath in files_to_fix_indent:
        if os.path.exists(filepath):
            fix_json_indentation(filepath)
        else:
            print(f"Warning: File not found: {filepath}")
    
    # Add final newline to the third file
    newline_file = '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'"'"'
    if os.path.exists(newline_file):
        add_final_newline(newline_file)
    else:
        print(f"Warning: File not found: {newline_file}")
    
    print("\nAll fixes applied!")
    return 0

if __name__ == '"'"'__main__'"'"':
    sys.exit(main())

    21	# Define the path to the [editorconfig-checker][1] executable.
    22	#
    23	# To install editorconfig-checker:
    24	#
    25	# ```bash
    26	# $ npm install editorconfig-checker
    27	# ```
    28	#
    29	# [1]: https://editorconfig-checker.github.io
    30	EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER ?= $(BIN_DIR)/editorconfig-checker
    31	
    32	# Define the path to the editorconfig-checker configuration file:
    33	EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_CONF ?= $(CONFIG_DIR)/editorconfig-checker/.editorconfig_checker.json
    34	
    35	# Define the path to the editorconfig-checker configuration file for Markdown files:
    36	EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_MARKDOWN_CONF ?= $(CONFIG_DIR)/editorconfig-checker/.editorconfig_checker.markdown.json
    37	
    38	# Define the output format (default is unset, which uses editorconfig-checker's default format)
    39	EDITORCONFIG_FORMAT ?=
    40	
    41	# Add the format flag if EDITORCONFIG_FORMAT is set
    42	EDITORCONFIG_FORMAT_FLAG := $(if $(EDITORCONFIG_FORMAT),--format=$(EDITORCONFIG_FORMAT))
    43	
    44	# Define the command-line options to use when invoking the editorconfig-checker executable:
    45	EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_CONF_FLAGS ?= \
    46	        --ignore-defaults \
    47	        $(EDITORCONFIG_FORMAT_FLAG)
    48	
    49	
    50	# RULES #
    51	
    52	#/
    53	# Lints files to ensure compliance with EditorConfig settings.
    54	#
    55	# @param {string} [PACKAGES_FILTER] - file path pattern (e.g., `.*/math/base/special/abs/.*`)
    56	#
    57	# @example
    58	# make lint-editorconfig
    59	#
    60	# @example
    61	# make lint-editorconfig PACKAGES_FILTER=".*/math/base/special/abs/.*"
    62	#/
    63	lint-editorconfig: $(NODE_MODULES)
    64	        $(QUIET) $(FIND_PACKAGES_CMD) | grep '^[\/]\|^[a-zA-Z]:[/\]' | while read -r pkg; do \
    65	                echo ''; \
    66	                echo "Linting package for basic formatting errors: $$pkg"; \
    67	                cd "$$pkg" && ( $(NODE) $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER) $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_CONF_FLAGS) --config $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_CONF) ./ && $(NODE) $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER) $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_CONF_FLAGS) --config $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_MARKDOWN_CONF) ./ && echo 'Success. No detected EditorConfig lint errors.' && echo '' ) || exit 1; \
    68	        done
    69	
    70	.PHONY: lint-editorconfig
    71	
    72	#/
    73	# Lints a specified list of files to ensure compliance with EditorConfig settings.
    74	#
    75	# ## Notes
    76	#
    77	# -   This rule is useful when wanting to lint a list of files generated by some other command (e.g., a list of changed files obtained via `git diff`).
    78	#
    79	# @private
    80	# @param {string} FILES - list of file paths
    81	#
    82	# @example
    83	# make lint-editorconfig-files FILES='foo/test.js bar/index.d.ts'
    84	#/
    85	lint-editorconfig-files: $(NODE_MODULES)
    86	        $(QUIET) $(DELETE) $(DELETE_FLAGS) "$(BUILD_DIR)/editorconfig-checker"
    87	        $(QUIET) echo 'Linting files for basic formatting errors...'
    88	        $(QUIET) $(MKDIR_RECURSIVE) "$(BUILD_DIR)/editorconfig-checker"
    89	        $(QUIET) echo $(FILES) | tr ' ' '\n' | $(TAR) -cf - -T - | $(TAR) -xf - -C "$(BUILD_DIR)/editorconfig-checker/"
    90	        $(QUIET) cd "$(BUILD_DIR)/editorconfig-checker" && \
    91	                $(NODE) $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER) $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_CONF_FLAGS) --config $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_CONF) ./ && \
    92	                $(NODE) $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER) $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_CONF_FLAGS) --config $(EDITORCONFIG_CHECKER_MARKDOWN_CONF) ./ && \
    93	                echo 'Success. No detected EditorConfig lint errors.' && \
    94	                echo ''
    95	
    96	.PHONY: lint-editorconfig-files

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/comprehensive_test.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Comprehensive test to verify EditorConfig fixes."""

import json
import sys
import os

def test_json_file_validity(filepath):
    """Test that the JSON file is still valid after fixing."""
    try:
        with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
            json.load(f)
        print(f"✓ {filepath}: Valid JSON")
        return True
    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Invalid JSON - {e}")
        return False

def test_indentation(filepath, expected_indent_style='"'"'space'"'"', expected_indent_size=2):
    """Test that indentation is correct."""
    with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        lines = f.readlines()
    
    errors = []
    for i, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
        # Skip empty lines
        if not line.strip():
            continue
        
        # Check for tabs vs spaces at the start of the line
        if line.startswith('"'"'\t'"'"'):
            if expected_indent_style == '"'"'space'"'"':
                errors.append(f"Line {i}: Found tab, expected {expected_indent_size} spaces")
        elif line.startswith('"'"' '"'"'):
            if expected_indent_style == '"'"'tab'"'"':
                errors.append(f"Line {i}: Found space(s), expected tab")
    
    if errors:
        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Indentation errors found")
        for error in errors[:3]:
            print(f"    {error}")
        return False
    else:
        print(f"✓ {filepath}: Correct indentation ({expected_indent_style})")
        return True

def test_final_newline(filepath):
    """Test that file ends with a newline."""
    with open(filepath, '"'"'rb'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    if content and content.endswith(b'"'"'\n'"'"'):
        print(f"✓ {filepath}: Has final newline")
        return True
    else:
        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Missing final newline")
        return False

def test_line_endings(filepath):
    """Test that file uses LF line endings."""
    with open(filepath, '"'"'rb'"'"') as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Check for CRLF
    if b'"'"'\r\n'"'"' in content:
        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Contains CRLF line endings (should be LF)")
        return False
    
    # Check for CR only
    if b'"'"'\r'"'"' in content:
        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Contains CR line endings (should be LF)")
        return False
    
    print(f"✓ {filepath}: Uses LF line endings")
    return True

def main():
    files_to_test = [
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"',
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"',
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'"'"'
    ]
    
    all_passed = True
    
    for filepath in files_to_test:
        print(f"\n{'"'"'='"'"'*70}")
        print(f"Testing: {os.path.basename(filepath)}")
        print('"'"'='"'"'*70)
        
        if not os.path.exists(filepath):
            print(f"✗ File not found: {filepath}")
            all_passed = False
            continue
        
        # Run all tests
        tests = [
            test_json_file_validity(filepath),
            test_indentation(filepath),
            test_final_newline(filepath),
            test_line_endings(filepath)
        ]
        
        if not all(tests):
            all_passed = False
    
    print(f"\n{'"'"'='"'"'*70}")
    if all_passed:
        print("✓ All tests passed!")
        return 0
    else:
        print("✗ Some tests failed!")
        return 1

if __name__ == '"'"'__main__'"'"':
    sys.exit(main())

"""
Simulate the exact error checking from the EditorConfig lint workflow.
This mimics what the actual linter was checking for.
"""

import sys

def check_file(filepath, description):
    """Check a file for EditorConfig compliance issues."""
    errors = []
    
    with open(filepath, '"'"'rb'"'"') as f:
        lines = f.readlines()
    
    # Check each line for wrong indent style
    for i, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
        if line.strip():  # Skip empty lines
            # For JSON files, check if tabs are used instead of spaces
            if line.startswith(b'"'"'\t'"'"'):
                errors.append(f"{i}: Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)")
    
    # Check for final newline
    if lines and not lines[-1].endswith(b'"'"'\n'"'"'):
        errors.append("Wrong line endings or no final newline")
    
    return errors

def main():
    # The three files mentioned in the PR description
    files_to_check = [
        ('"'"'lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"', 
         '"'"'defaults.json'"'"'),
        ('"'"'lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"',
         '"'"'ignore_patterns.json'"'"'),
        ('"'"'lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'"'"',
         '"'"'medium_positive_5.json'"'"')
    ]
    
    total_errors = 0
    print("Linting files for basic formatting errors...")
    
    for filepath, description in files_to_check:
        errors = check_file(filepath, description)
        
        if errors:
            print(f"{filepath}:")
            # Group consecutive line errors
            line_errors = [e for e in errors if '"'"':'"'"' in e and '"'"'Wrong indent'"'"' in e]
            other_errors = [e for e in errors if e not in line_errors]
            
            if line_errors:
                # Extract line numbers
                line_nums = [int(e.split('"'"':'"'"')[0]) for e in line_errors]
                if line_nums:
                    min_line = min(line_nums)
                    max_line = max(line_nums)
                    print(f"\t{min_line}-{max_line}: Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)")
            
            for error in other_errors:
                print(f"\t{error}")
            
            total_errors += len(errors)
    
    if total_errors > 0:
        print(f"\n{total_errors} errors found")
        return 1
    else:
        print("\n0 errors found")
        print("✓ All files pass EditorConfig linting!")
        return 0

if __name__ == '"'"'__main__'"'"':
    sys.exit(main())
'

"""
Edge case testing to ensure robustness of fixes.
"""

import sys
import json

def test_json_parsing():
    """Test that JSON files can still be parsed correctly."""
    files = [
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"',
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"',

        try:
            with open(filepath, '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            print(f"✓ {filepath.split('"'"'/'"'"')[-1]}: Successfully parsed")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"✗ {filepath.split('"'"'/'"'"')[-1]}: Failed to parse - {e}")
            return False
    
    return True

def test_content_integrity():
    """Test that the content hasn'"'"'t been corrupted."""
    # Test defaults.json has all expected keys
    with open('"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        defaults = json.load(f)
    
    expected_keys = {'"'"'protocol'"'"', '"'"'hostname'"'"', '"'"'port'"'"', '"'"'pathname'"'"', '"'"'page'"'"', 
                     '"'"'last_page'"'"', '"'"'per_page'"'"', '"'"'query'"'"', '"'"'method'"'"', '"'"'useragent'"'"', '"'"'accept'"'"'}
    
    if set(defaults.keys()) == expected_keys:
        print("✓ defaults.json: All expected keys present")
    else:
        print(f"✗ defaults.json: Key mismatch")
        print(f"  Expected: {expected_keys}")
        print(f"  Got: {set(defaults.keys())}")
        return False
    
    # Test ignore_patterns.json is an array
    with open('"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        patterns = json.load(f)
    
    if isinstance(patterns, list) and len(patterns) > 0:
        print(f"✓ ignore_patterns.json: Valid array with {len(patterns)} entries")
    else:
        print(f"✗ ignore_patterns.json: Invalid structure")
        return False
    
    # Test medium_positive_5.json has required structure
    with open('"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'"'"', '"'"'r'"'"') as f:
        data = json.load(f)
    
    if '"'"'n'"'"' in data and '"'"'x'"'"' in data and '"'"'expected'"'"' in data:
        if data['"'"'n'"'"'] == 5 and len(data['"'"'x'"'"']) == len(data['"'"'expected'"'"']):
            print(f"✓ medium_positive_5.json: Valid structure (n={data['"'"'n'"'"']}, {len(data['"'"'x'"'"'])} values)")
        else:
            print(f"✗ medium_positive_5.json: Data mismatch")
            return False
    else:
        print(f"✗ medium_positive_5.json: Missing required keys")
        return False
    
    return True

def test_no_mixed_indentation():
    """Test that files don'"'"'t have mixed tabs and spaces."""
    files = [
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json'"'"',
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'"'"',
        '"'"'/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'"'"'
    ]
    
    print("\nTesting for mixed indentation...")
    for filepath in files:
        with open(filepath, '"'"'rb'"'"') as f:
            content = f.read()
        
        # Count tabs and leading spaces
        lines = content.split(b'"'"'\n'"'"')
        has_tab_indent = any(line.startswith(b'"'"'\t'"'"') for line in lines)
        has_space_indent = any(line.startswith(b'"'"'  '"'"') for line in lines)  # 2+ spaces
        
        if has_tab_indent and has_space_indent:
            print(f"✗ {filepath.split('"'"'/'"'"')[-1]}: Has mixed indentation")
            return False
        elif has_tab_indent:
            print(f"✗ {filepath.split('"'"'/'"'"')[-1]}: Uses tabs (should use spaces)")
            return False
        else:
            print(f"✓ {filepath.split('"'"'/'"'"')[-1]}: Consistent indentation")
    
    return True

    print("="*70)
    print("EDGE CASE TESTING")
    print("="*70)
    print()
    
    all_passed = True
    
    # Test 1: JSON parsing
    if not test_json_parsing():

        print("✓ ALL EDGE CASE TESTS PASSED!")
        return 0
    else:
        print("✗ SOME EDGE CASE TESTS FAILED!")
        return 1

if __name__ == '"'"'__main__'"'"':
    sys.exit(main())

## Problem Description

The EditorConfig lint workflow detected 3 errors in the repository:

1. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json**
   - Lines 2-12: Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)

2. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json**
   - Lines 2-100: Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)

3. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json**
   - Wrong line endings or no final newline

## Root Cause

According to the `.editorconfig` file in the repository root:
- JSON files should use **spaces** for indentation (indent_size = 2)
- All files should end with a newline (insert_final_newline = true)

The three problematic files had:
1. Used tabs instead of 2 spaces for indentation (files 1 & 2)
2. Missing final newline character (file 3)

## Solution Implemented

### Files Modified

1. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json**
   - Replaced all tab characters with 2 spaces
   - Result: 11 lines of properly indented JSON

2. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json**
   - Replaced all tab characters with 2 spaces
   - Result: 99 array entries properly indented

3. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json**
   - Added final newline character at end of file
   - Result: File now ends with '"'"'\n'"'"' as required

### Changes Made

The fix was implemented by:
1. Reading each file'"'"'s content
2. Replacing tab characters ('"'"'\t'"'"') with two spaces ('"'"'  '"'"')
3. Ensuring files end with a newline character ('"'"'\n'"'"')

### Verification

All fixes were verified to:
- ✓ Pass EditorConfig compliance checks
- ✓ Maintain valid JSON syntax
- ✓ Preserve original data and structure
- ✓ Use consistent indentation (no mixed tabs/spaces)
- ✓ Have proper line endings (LF)
- ✓ End with a newline character

## Testing

1. JSON validity and parseability
2. Correct indentation style (spaces not tabs)
3. Presence of final newline
4. Content integrity (no data loss)
5. No mixed indentation
6. Proper LF line endings

All tests passed successfully.

## Impact

These are minimal formatting changes that:
- Do NOT change the functionality of the code
- Do NOT modify any test logic or data
- Do NOT affect runtime behavior
- Only ensure compliance with project'"'"'s EditorConfig standards

The JSON files remain valid and their data is unchanged.

import sys

# Simulate the exact check that would have failed before our fix
files_to_check = [
    'lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json',
    'lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json',
    'lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'
]

print('Linting files for basic formatting errors...')
errors = 0

for filepath in files_to_check:
    with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
        content = f.read()
        lines = content.split(b'\n')
    
    # Check for tabs in indentation
    tab_lines = []
    for i, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
        if line.startswith(b'\t'):
            tab_lines.append(i)
    
    if tab_lines:
        print(f'{filepath}:')
        if len(tab_lines) > 1:
            print(f'	{tab_lines[0]}-{tab_lines[-1]}: Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)')
        else:
            print(f'	{tab_lines[0]}: Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)')
        errors += len(tab_lines)
    
    # Check for final newline
    if content and not content.endswith(b'\n'):
        if not tab_lines:  # Only print filename if not already printed
            print(f'{filepath}:')
        print(f'	Wrong line endings or no final newline')
        errors += 1

if errors > 0:
    print(f'\n{errors} errors found')
    sys.exit(1)
else:
    print('\n0 errors found')
    print('Success. No detected EditorConfig lint errors.')
    sys.exit(0)

+# EditorConfig Lint Errors - Fix Summary
+
+## Problem Description
+
+The EditorConfig lint workflow detected 3 errors in the repository:
+
+1. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json**
+   - Lines 2-12: Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)
+
+2. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json**
+   - Lines 2-100: Wrong indent style found (tabs instead of spaces)
+
+3. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json**
+   - Wrong line endings or no final newline
+
+## Root Cause
+
+According to the `.editorconfig` file in the repository root:
+- JSON files should use **spaces** for indentation (indent_size = 2)
+- All files should end with a newline (insert_final_newline = true)
+
+The three problematic files had:
+1. Used tabs instead of 2 spaces for indentation (files 1 & 2)
+2. Missing final newline character (file 3)
+
+## Solution Implemented
+
+### Files Modified
+
+1. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json**
+   - Replaced all tab characters with 2 spaces
+   - Result: 11 lines of properly indented JSON
+
+2. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json**
+   - Replaced all tab characters with 2 spaces
+   - Result: 99 array entries properly indented
+
+3. **lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json**
+   - Added final newline character at end of file
+   - Result: File now ends with '\n' as required
+
+### Changes Made
+
+The fix was implemented by:
+1. Reading each file's content
+2. Replacing tab characters ('\t') with two spaces ('  ')
+3. Ensuring files end with a newline character ('\n')
+
+### Verification
+
+All fixes were verified to:
+- ✓ Pass EditorConfig compliance checks
+- ✓ Maintain valid JSON syntax
+- ✓ Preserve original data and structure
+- ✓ Use consistent indentation (no mixed tabs/spaces)
+- ✓ Have proper line endings (LF)
+- ✓ End with a newline character
+
+## Testing
+
+Multiple test scripts were created and run to verify:
+1. JSON validity and parseability
+2. Correct indentation style (spaces not tabs)
+3. Presence of final newline
+4. Content integrity (no data loss)
+5. No mixed indentation
+6. Proper LF line endings
+
+All tests passed successfully.
+
+## Impact
+
+These are minimal formatting changes that:
+- Do NOT change the functionality of the code
+- Do NOT modify any test logic or data
+- Do NOT affect runtime behavior
+- Only ensure compliance with project's EditorConfig standards
+
+The JSON files remain valid and their data is unchanged.

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Script to check EditorConfig compliance for the three problematic files."""
+
+import sys
+import os
+
+def check_file_indentation(filepath, expected_indent_style, expected_indent_size=None):
+    """Check if a file uses the correct indentation style."""
+    errors = []
+    
+    with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
+        lines = f.readlines()
+    
+    for i, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
+        # Skip empty lines
+        if not line.strip():
+            continue
+        
+        # Check for tabs vs spaces at the start of the line
+        if line.startswith(b'\t'):
+            if expected_indent_style == 'space':
+                errors.append(f"Line {i}: Found tab, expected {expected_indent_size} spaces")
+        elif line.startswith(b' '):
+            if expected_indent_style == 'tab':
+                errors.append(f"Line {i}: Found space(s), expected tab")
+    
+    return errors
+
+def check_file_newline(filepath):
+    """Check if a file ends with a newline."""
+    with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
+        f.seek(0, 2)  # Go to end
+        if f.tell() > 0:
+            f.seek(-1, 2)  # Go to last byte
+            last_char = f.read(1)
+            return last_char == b'\n'
+    return True
+
+def main():
+    files_to_check = [
+        {
+            'path': '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json',
+            'indent_style': 'space',
+            'indent_size': 2
+        },
+        {
+            'path': '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json',
+            'indent_style': 'space',
+            'indent_size': 2
+        },
+        {
+            'path': '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json',
+            'indent_style': 'space',  # JSON files should use spaces
+            'indent_size': 2,
+            'check_newline': True
+        }
+    ]
+    
+    all_errors = []
+    
+    for file_info in files_to_check:
+        filepath = file_info['path']
+        
+        if not os.path.exists(filepath):
+            print(f"Warning: File not found: {filepath}")
+            continue
+        
+        print(f"\nChecking: {filepath}")
+        
+        # Check indentation
+        errors = check_file_indentation(
+            filepath,
+            file_info['indent_style'],
+            file_info.get('indent_size')
+        )
+        
+        if errors:
+            print(f"  Indentation errors: {len(errors)}")
+            for error in errors[:5]:  # Show first 5 errors
+                print(f"    - {error}")
+            if len(errors) > 5:
+                print(f"    ... and {len(errors) - 5} more")
+            all_errors.extend(errors)
+        else:
+            print("  ✓ Indentation OK")
+        
+        # Check newline
+        if file_info.get('check_newline'):
+            has_newline = check_file_newline(filepath)
+            if not has_newline:
+                print("  ✗ Missing final newline")
+                all_errors.append(f"{filepath}: Missing final newline")
+            else:
+                print("  ✓ Final newline OK")
+    
+    print(f"\n{'='*60}")
+    if all_errors:
+        print(f"Total errors found: {len(all_errors)}")
+        return 1
+    else:
+        print("All files pass EditorConfig checks!")
+        return 0
+
+if __name__ == '__main__':
+    sys.exit(main())

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Comprehensive test to verify EditorConfig fixes."""
+
+import json
+import sys
+import os
+
+def test_json_file_validity(filepath):
+    """Test that the JSON file is still valid after fixing."""
+    try:
+        with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+            json.load(f)
+        print(f"✓ {filepath}: Valid JSON")
+        return True
+    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
+        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Invalid JSON - {e}")
+        return False
+
+def test_indentation(filepath, expected_indent_style='space', expected_indent_size=2):
+    """Test that indentation is correct."""
+    with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+        lines = f.readlines()
+    
+    errors = []
+    for i, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
+        # Skip empty lines
+        if not line.strip():
+            continue
+        
+        # Check for tabs vs spaces at the start of the line
+        if line.startswith('\t'):
+            if expected_indent_style == 'space':
+                errors.append(f"Line {i}: Found tab, expected {expected_indent_size} spaces")
+        elif line.startswith(' '):
+            if expected_indent_style == 'tab':
+                errors.append(f"Line {i}: Found space(s), expected tab")
+    
+    if errors:
+        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Indentation errors found")
+        for error in errors[:3]:
+            print(f"    {error}")
+        return False
+    else:
+        print(f"✓ {filepath}: Correct indentation ({expected_indent_style})")
+        return True
+
+def test_final_newline(filepath):
+    """Test that file ends with a newline."""
+    with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+    
+    if content and content.endswith(b'\n'):
+        print(f"✓ {filepath}: Has final newline")
+        return True
+    else:
+        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Missing final newline")
+        return False
+
+def test_line_endings(filepath):
+    """Test that file uses LF line endings."""
+    with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+    
+    # Check for CRLF
+    if b'\r\n' in content:
+        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Contains CRLF line endings (should be LF)")
+        return False
+    
+    # Check for CR only
+    if b'\r' in content:
+        print(f"✗ {filepath}: Contains CR line endings (should be LF)")
+        return False
+    
+    print(f"✓ {filepath}: Uses LF line endings")
+    return True
+
+def main():
+    files_to_test = [
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json',
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json',
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'
+    ]
+    
+    all_passed = True
+    
+    for filepath in files_to_test:
+        print(f"\n{'='*70}")
+        print(f"Testing: {os.path.basename(filepath)}")
+        print('='*70)
+        
+        if not os.path.exists(filepath):
+            print(f"✗ File not found: {filepath}")
+            all_passed = False
+            continue
+        
+        # Run all tests
+        tests = [
+            test_json_file_validity(filepath),
+            test_indentation(filepath),
+            test_final_newline(filepath),
+            test_line_endings(filepath)
+        ]
+        
+        if not all(tests):
+            all_passed = False
+    
+    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
+    if all_passed:
+        print("✓ All tests passed!")
+        return 0
+    else:
+        print("✗ Some tests failed!")
+        return 1
+
+if __name__ == '__main__':
+    sys.exit(main())

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Edge case testing to ensure robustness of fixes.
+"""
+
+import sys
+import json
+
+def test_json_parsing():
+    """Test that JSON files can still be parsed correctly."""
+    files = [
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json',
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json',
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'
+    ]
+    
+    print("Testing JSON parsing after fixes...")
+    for filepath in files:
+        try:
+            with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+                data = json.load(f)
+            print(f"✓ {filepath.split('/')[-1]}: Successfully parsed")
+        except Exception as e:
+            print(f"✗ {filepath.split('/')[-1]}: Failed to parse - {e}")
+            return False
+    
+    return True
+
+def test_content_integrity():
+    """Test that the content hasn't been corrupted."""
+    # Test defaults.json has all expected keys
+    with open('/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json', 'r') as f:
+        defaults = json.load(f)
+    
+    expected_keys = {'protocol', 'hostname', 'port', 'pathname', 'page', 
+                     'last_page', 'per_page', 'query', 'method', 'useragent', 'accept'}
+    
+    if set(defaults.keys()) == expected_keys:
+        print("✓ defaults.json: All expected keys present")
+    else:
+        print(f"✗ defaults.json: Key mismatch")
+        print(f"  Expected: {expected_keys}")
+        print(f"  Got: {set(defaults.keys())}")
+        return False
+    
+    # Test ignore_patterns.json is an array
+    with open('/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json', 'r') as f:
+        patterns = json.load(f)
+    
+    if isinstance(patterns, list) and len(patterns) > 0:
+        print(f"✓ ignore_patterns.json: Valid array with {len(patterns)} entries")
+    else:
+        print(f"✗ ignore_patterns.json: Invalid structure")
+        return False
+    
+    # Test medium_positive_5.json has required structure
+    with open('/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json', 'r') as f:
+        data = json.load(f)
+    
+    if 'n' in data and 'x' in data and 'expected' in data:
+        if data['n'] == 5 and len(data['x']) == len(data['expected']):
+            print(f"✓ medium_positive_5.json: Valid structure (n={data['n']}, {len(data['x'])} values)")
+        else:
+            print(f"✗ medium_positive_5.json: Data mismatch")
+            return False
+    else:
+        print(f"✗ medium_positive_5.json: Missing required keys")
+        return False
+    
+    return True
+
+def test_no_mixed_indentation():
+    """Test that files don't have mixed tabs and spaces."""
+    files = [
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json',
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json',
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'
+    ]
+    
+    print("\nTesting for mixed indentation...")
+    for filepath in files:
+        with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
+            content = f.read()
+        
+        # Count tabs and leading spaces
+        lines = content.split(b'\n')
+        has_tab_indent = any(line.startswith(b'\t') for line in lines)
+        has_space_indent = any(line.startswith(b'  ') for line in lines)  # 2+ spaces
+        
+        if has_tab_indent and has_space_indent:
+            print(f"✗ {filepath.split('/')[-1]}: Has mixed indentation")
+            return False
+        elif has_tab_indent:
+            print(f"✗ {filepath.split('/')[-1]}: Uses tabs (should use spaces)")
+            return False
+        else:
+            print(f"✓ {filepath.split('/')[-1]}: Consistent indentation")
+    
+    return True
+
+def main():
+    print("="*70)
+    print("EDGE CASE TESTING")
+    print("="*70)
+    print()
+    
+    all_passed = True
+    
+    # Test 1: JSON parsing
+    if not test_json_parsing():
+        all_passed = False
+    
+    print()
+    
+    # Test 2: Content integrity
+    if not test_content_integrity():
+        all_passed = False
+    
+    print()
+    
+    # Test 3: No mixed indentation
+    if not test_no_mixed_indentation():
+        all_passed = False
+    
+    print()
+    print("="*70)
+    if all_passed:
+        print("✓ ALL EDGE CASE TESTS PASSED!")
+        return 0
+    else:
+        print("✗ SOME EDGE CASE TESTS FAILED!")
+        return 1
+
+if __name__ == '__main__':
+    sys.exit(main())

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Script to fix EditorConfig issues in the three problematic files."""
+
+import sys
+import os
+
+def fix_json_indentation(filepath):
+    """Fix indentation in a JSON file to use 2 spaces instead of tabs."""
+    with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+    
+    # Replace tabs with 2 spaces
+    fixed_content = content.replace('\t', '  ')
+    
+    with open(filepath, 'w') as f:
+        f.write(fixed_content)
+    
+    print(f"Fixed indentation in: {filepath}")
+
+def add_final_newline(filepath):
+    """Ensure file ends with a newline."""
+    with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+    
+    if content and not content.endswith(b'\n'):
+        with open(filepath, 'ab') as f:
+            f.write(b'\n')
+        print(f"Added final newline to: {filepath}")
+    else:
+        print(f"Already has final newline: {filepath}")
+
+def main():
+    # Fix indentation in the two JSON files
+    files_to_fix_indent = [
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/github/user-repos/lib/defaults.json',
+        '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/_tools/lint/filenames/lib/ignore_patterns.json'
+    ]
+    
+    for filepath in files_to_fix_indent:
+        if os.path.exists(filepath):
+            fix_json_indentation(filepath)
+        else:
+            print(f"Warning: File not found: {filepath}")
+    
+    # Add final newline to the third file
+    newline_file = '/testbed/lib/node_modules/@stdlib/math/base/tools/normhermitepolyf/test/fixtures/python/medium_positive_5.json'
+    if os.path.exists(newline_file):
+        add_final_newline(newline_file)
+    else:
+        print(f"Warning: File not found: {newline_file}")
+    
+    print("\nAll fixes applied!")
+    return 0
+
+if __name__ == '__main__':
+    sys.exit(main())
